          "When Neris Vale returns to Oathstone Causeway, it becomes obvious that ash, oath-smoke, and ancestral pressure cling to every threshold.           "In the catacombs, Caelan reveals furnace records listing each life traded into the mountain wards. Neris wants to expose Maeron immediately, yet doing so before the warding rite could leave the valley open to the winter breach. The chapter keeps faith with identity-self under reconciliation pressure while moving toward cliffhanger, and it refuses relief without visible cost.
